msg:Exceptional hotel with prime location for fair visiting.  Connected to the Expo Complex with footbridge on 3/F.  I was given a corner room with 270 degrees view of the city for one night.  Room service was delicious and just what I needed to recharge after a full day of booth browsing.  Buffet breakfast was outstanding and plenty to keep me going for the rest of the day without lunch. Westin had an exclusive golf cart shuttle across the footbridge but unfortunately no driver was available during my stay.  Overall I'd rate this hotel 95/100 and will definitely return for the next fair.
